<p><b>Indonesia</b>,<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-14"><a href="#cite_note-14">[a]</a></sup> officially the <b>Republic of Indonesia</b>,<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-fn1_15-0"><a href="#cite_note-fn1-15">[b]</a></sup> is a country in <a href="/wiki/Southeast_Asia" title="Southeast Asia">Southeast Asia</a> and <a href="/wiki/Oceania" title="Oceania">Oceania</a> between the <a href="/wiki/Indian_Ocean" title="Indian Ocean">Indian</a> and <a href="/wiki/Pacific_Ocean" title="Pacific Ocean">Pacific</a> oceans. It consists of over <a href="/wiki/List_of_islands_of_Indonesia" title="List of islands of Indonesia">17,000 islands</a>, including <a href="/wiki/Sumatra" title="Sumatra">Sumatra</a>, <a href="/wiki/Java" title="Java">Java</a>, <a href="/wiki/Sulawesi" title="Sulawesi">Sulawesi</a>, and parts of <a href="/wiki/Borneo" title="Borneo">Borneo</a> and <a href="/wiki/New_Guinea" title="New Guinea">New Guinea</a>. Indonesia is the world's largest <a href="/wiki/Archipelagic_state" title="Archipelagic state">archipelagic state</a> and the <a href="/wiki/List_of_countries_and_dependencies_by_area" title="List of countries and dependencies by area">14th-largest country by area</a>, at 1,904,569 square kilometres (735,358 <a href="/wiki/Square_mile" title="Square mile">square miles</a>). With over 275 million people, Indonesia is the world's <a href="/wiki/List_of_countries_and_dependencies_by_population" title="List of countries and dependencies by population">fourth-most populous country</a> and the most populous <a href="/wiki/Islam_by_country" title="Islam by country">Muslim-majority country</a>. Java, the world's <a href="/wiki/List_of_islands_by_population" title="List of islands by population">most populous island</a>, is home to more than half of the country's population.
</p><p>Indonesia is a <a href="/wiki/President_of_Indonesia" title="President of Indonesia">presidential</a> <a href="/wiki/Republic" title="Republic">republic</a> with an elected <a href="/wiki/People%27s_Consultative_Assembly" title="People's Consultative Assembly">legislature</a>. It has <a href="/wiki/Provinces_of_Indonesia" title="Provinces of Indonesia">37 provinces</a>, of which eight have <a href="/wiki/Autonomous_administrative_division" title="Autonomous administrative division">special status</a>. The country's capital, <a href="/wiki/Jakarta" title="Jakarta">Jakarta</a>, is the world's <a href="/wiki/List_of_largest_cities" title="List of largest cities">second-most populous urban area</a>. Indonesia shares <a href="/wiki/Template:Borders_of_Indonesia" title="Template:Borders of Indonesia">land borders</a> with <a href="/wiki/Papua_New_Guinea" title="Papua New Guinea">Papua New Guinea</a>, <a href="/wiki/East_Timor" title="East Timor">East Timor</a>, and the <a href="/wiki/East_Malaysia" title="East Malaysia">eastern part</a> of <a href="/wiki/Malaysia" title="Malaysia">Malaysia</a>, as well as <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Maritime_border" title="Maritime border">maritime borders</a> with <a href="/wiki/Singapore" title="Singapore">Singapore</a>, <a href="/wiki/Vietnam" title="Vietnam">Vietnam</a>, <a href="/wiki/Thailand" title="Thailand">Thailand</a>, the <a href="/wiki/Philippines" title="Philippines">Philippines</a>, <a href="/wiki/Australia" title="Australia">Australia</a>, <a href="/wiki/Palau" title="Palau">Palau</a>, and <a href="/wiki/India" title="India">India</a> (<a href="/wiki/Andaman_and_Nicobar_Islands" title="Andaman and Nicobar Islands">Andaman and Nicobar Islands</a>). Despite its large population and densely populated regions, Indonesia has vast areas of wilderness that support one of the <a href="/wiki/Megadiverse_countries" title="Megadiverse countries">world's highest levels of biodiversity</a>.
</p><p>The <a href="/wiki/Nusantara_(archipelago)" title="Nusantara (archipelago)">Indonesian archipelago</a> has been a valuable region for trade since at least the 7th century when <a href="/wiki/Srivijaya" title="Srivijaya">Srivijaya</a> and later <a href="/wiki/Majapahit" title="Majapahit">Majapahit</a> traded with entities from <a href="/wiki/Mainland_China" title="Mainland China">mainland China</a> and the <a href="/wiki/Indian_subcontinent" title="Indian subcontinent">Indian subcontinent</a>. Local rulers gradually absorbed foreign influences from the early centuries, and <a href="/wiki/Hinduism_in_Indonesia" title="Hinduism in Indonesia">Hindu</a> and <a href="/wiki/Buddhism_in_Indonesia" title="Buddhism in Indonesia">Buddhist</a> kingdoms flourished. <a href="/wiki/Sunni_Islam" title="Sunni Islam">Sunni</a> traders and <a href="/wiki/Sufism" title="Sufism">Sufi</a> scholars brought <a href="/wiki/Islam_in_Indonesia" title="Islam in Indonesia">Islam</a>, while <a href="/wiki/Christianity_in_Indonesia" title="Christianity in Indonesia">Christianity</a> was spread by European missionaries. Although the <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Portuguese_colonialism_in_the_East_Indies" title="Portuguese colonialism in the East Indies">Portuguese</a>, the <a href="/wiki/French_and_British_interregnum_in_the_Dutch_East_Indies" title="French and British interregnum in the Dutch East Indies">French and British</a> also ruled at some point, the <a href="/wiki/Dutch_East_Indies#History" title="Dutch East Indies">Dutch</a> were the foremost <a href="/wiki/Dutch_Empire" title="Dutch Empire">colonial power</a> for much of their 350-year presence in the archipelago. The concept of "Indonesia" as a nation-state <a href="/wiki/Indonesian_National_Awakening" title="Indonesian National Awakening">emerged</a> in the early 20th century, culminating later in the <a href="/wiki/Proclamation_of_Indonesian_Independence" title="Proclamation of Indonesian Independence">proclamation of Indonesian Independence</a> in 1945. However, it was not until 1949 that the Dutch recognised <a href="/wiki/United_States_of_Indonesia" title="United States of Indonesia">Indonesia's sovereignty</a> following an <a href="/wiki/Indonesian_National_Revolution" title="Indonesian National Revolution">armed and diplomatic conflict</a> between the two.
</p><p>Indonesia consists of thousands of <a href="/wiki/Ethnic_groups_in_Indonesia" title="Ethnic groups in Indonesia">distinct native ethnic</a> and hundreds of <a href="/wiki/Languages_of_Indonesia" title="Languages of Indonesia">linguistic</a> groups, with <a href="/wiki/Javanese_people" title="Javanese people">Javanese</a> being the largest. A shared identity has developed with the motto <i>"<a href="/wiki/Bhinneka_Tunggal_Ika" title="Bhinneka Tunggal Ika">Bhinneka Tunggal Ika</a>"</i> ("Unity in Diversity" <i>literally</i>, "many, yet one"), defined by a <a href="/wiki/Indonesian_language" title="Indonesian language">national language</a>, cultural diversity, religious pluralism within a Muslim-majority population, and a history of colonialism and rebellion against it. The <a href="/wiki/Economy_of_Indonesia" title="Economy of Indonesia">economy of Indonesia</a> is the world's <a href="/wiki/List_of_countries_by_GDP_(nominal)" title="List of countries by GDP (nominal)">17th-largest by nominal GDP</a> and the <a href="/wiki/List_of_countries_by_GDP_(PPP)" title="List of countries by GDP (PPP)">7th-largest by PPP</a>. It is a <a href="/wiki/Regional_power" title="Regional power">regional power</a> and is considered a <a href="/wiki/Middle_power" title="Middle power">middle power</a> in global affairs. The country is a member of several multilateral organisations, including the <a href="/wiki/United_Nations" title="United Nations">United Nations</a>, <a href="/wiki/World_Trade_Organization" title="World Trade Organization">World Trade Organization</a>, <a href="/wiki/G20" title="G20">G20</a>, and a founding member of the <a href="/wiki/Non-Aligned_Movement" title="Non-Aligned Movement">Non-Aligned Movement</a>, <a href="/wiki/ASEAN" title="ASEAN">Association of Southeast Asian Nations</a>, <a href="/wiki/East_Asia_Summit" title="East Asia Summit">East Asia Summit</a>, <a href="/wiki/D-8_Organization_for_Economic_Cooperation" title="D-8 Organization for Economic Cooperation">D-8</a> and the <a href="/wiki/Organisation_of_Islamic_Cooperation" title="Organisation of Islamic Cooperation">Organisation of Islamic Cooperation</a>.
</p>
